 Former Secretary of the Board of Control for Cricket in India JY Lele has died in Vadodara from a heart attack
 jayavant lele 75 saal ke the
 He is survived by his wife, son and a daughter
 guuruuvaar subah 11 baje unka antim sanskaar kiya jayega
 It is reported that his funeral may include Sachin Tendulkar and Sunil Gavaskar
 mukhar swabhaav ke lele bisisiai ke sahaayak sachiv or sachiv rahe jab jagmohan daalamia 1996 main isisi ke adhyaksh bane the
 He was associated with BCCI for nearly nine years
 unhone is dauraan kai ahm faisle liye
 In recent days, Lele has openly spoken against BCCI chief Srinivasan in IPL fixing
